3

一些人反对说，新税法不公平。
yī xiē rén fǎn duì shuō， xīn shuì fǎ bù gōng píng。
Some people objected that the new tax law was unfair.

一会儿工夫骚动平息了下来。
yī huìr gōng fu sāo dòng píng xī le xia lai。
Presently the tumult died down.

一场示威游行将要发生。
yī chǎng shì wēi yóu xíng jiāng yào fā shēng。
A disorderly demonstration will take place.

一片片的锈从旧铁锅上落下。
yī piàn piàn de xiù zòng jiù tiě guō shàng luò xià。
Flakes of rust are falling from the old iron pan.

一群人聚拢起来看发生了什么事。
yī qún rén jù lǒng qǐ lai kàn fā shēng le shén me shì。
A crowd gathered to see what had happened.

不断发展的经济使农民们富裕起来。
bù duàn fā zhǎn de jīng jì shǐ nóng mín men fù yù qǐ lai。
The expanding economy enriched the peasants.

不断增加的失业引起了社会骚乱。
bù duàn zēng jiā de shī yè yǐn qǐ le shè huì sāo luàn。
The increasing unemployment caused social unrest.

不要干涉别人的事情。
bù yào gān shè bié rén de shì qing。
Don't meddle with other men's business.

不要践踏草地。
bù yào jiàn tà cǎo dì。
Don't trample on the grass.

与其说她善良不如说她单纯。
yǔ qí shuō tā shàn liáng bù rú shuō tā dān chún。
She is not so kind as simple.

中国人民是一个勤劳的民族。
Zhōng guó rén mín shì yī gè qín láo de mín zú。
The Chinese are industrious people.

五月里各种植物鲜花盛开。
wǔ yuè lǐ gè zhǒng zhí wù xiān huā shèng kāi。
In May, all kinds of plants are in full bloom.

人应当倾听自己的内心感觉。
rén yīng dāng qīng tīng zì jǐ de nèi xīn gǎn jué。
He should listen to his intimate feelings.

人生幸福易逝。
rén shēng xìng fú yì shì。
Human happiness is so fragile.

人类是在幼年开始学习第一种语言的。
rén lèi shì zài yòu nián kāi shǐ xué xí dì yī zhòng yǔ yán de。
Mankind learns its first language in early childhood.

从资料库借磁带是退而求其次的办法。
zòng zī liào kù jiè cí dài shì tuì ér qiú qí cì de bàn fǎ。
Borrowing tapes from the library would be the next-best thing.

他不听母亲的劝告，参加了那次聚会。
tā bù tìng mǔ qīn de quàn gào， cān jiā le nà cì jù huì。
He disobeyed his mother and went to the party.

他不辞劳苦地学习英语。
tā bù cí láo kǔ de xué xí Yīng yǔ。
He spares no pains to study English.

他为什么到那里去，这对我来说是个谜。
tā wèi shén me dào nà li qù， zhè duì wǒ lái shuō shì gè mí。
Why he went there is a mystery to me.

他以两杆的成绩赢得了这场高尔夫球赛。
tā yǐ liǎng gǎn de chéng jī yíng dé le zhè chǎng gāo ěr fū qiú sài。
He won the golf match by two shots.

他以友谊为掩护欺骗了我们。
tā yǐ yǒu yì wèi yǎn hù qī piàn le wǒ men。
He cheated us under the guise of friendship.

他们俩在公园的长凳上拥抱亲吻。
tā men liǎng zài gōng yuán de zhǎng dèng shàng yōng bào qīn wěn。
The two of them were necking on a park bench.

他们决定结束彼此的关系.
tā men jué dìng jié shù bǐ cǐ de guān xi.
They decided to end their relationship.

他们在恶劣的天气条件下登上了山的顶峰。
tā men zài è liè de tiān qì tiáo jiàn xià dēng shàng le shān de dǐng fēng。
They climbed up the last part of the mountain in formidable weather conditions.

他们在碎石小径上散步。
tā men zài suì shí xiǎo jìng shàng sàn bù。
They went out for a walk on the gravelled path.

他们坐在凉亭里，边喝茶边聊天。
tā men zuò zài liáng tíng lǐ， biān hè chá biān liáo tiān。
They sat in the arbor and chatted over tea.

他们宁愿去钓鱼，也不愿待在家里。
tā men nìng yuàn qù diào yú， yě bù yuàn dài zài jiā lǐ。
They would rather go fishing than stay at home.

他们把火车的车厢连接好。
tā men bǎ huǒ chē de chē xiāng lián jiē hào。
They coupled the carriages of the train together.

他们标明每艘船的新位置。
tā men biāo míng měi sōu chuán de xīn wèi zhi。
They plotted the new position of each vessel.

他们用绳索把犯人捆起来。
tā men yòng shéng suǒ bǎ fàn rén kǔn qǐ lai。
They tied their prisoner up with a piece of rope.

他们衷心欢迎他。
tā men zhōng xīn huān yíng tā。
They gave him a hearty welcome.

他们要求对税收制度进行根本改革。
tā men yāo qiú duì shuì shōu zhì dù jìn xíng gēn běn gǎi gé。
They called for a radical reform of our tax system.

他们说说笑笑，沿着海滩散步。
tā men shuō shuō xiào xiào， yán zhe hǎi tān sàn bù。
They walked along the beach talking and laughing.

他公然蔑视上司，并要求他作出解释。
tā gōng rán miè shì shàng si， bìng yāo qiú tā zuò chū jiě shì。
He bearded his boss and demanded an explanation.

他关上了灯，室内一片漆黑。
tā guān shàng le dēng， shì nèi yī piàn qī hēi。
He turned off the light and the room was in complete darkness.

他向高脚酒杯里倒了一些葡萄酒。
tā xiàng gāo jué jiǔ bēi lǐ dào le yī xiē pú tao jiǔ。
He poured some wine into the goblet.

他呆在幕后为了避开公众的注意。
tā dāi zài mù hòu wèi le bì kāi gōng zhòng de zhù yì。
He stayed in the background to escape from the public attention.

他在密西西比河流域拥有一个大农场。
tā zài mì xī xī bì hé liú yù yōng yǒu yī gè dà nóng chǎng。
He has a large farm in the Mississippi Valley.

他在雪中漫步。
tā zài xuě zhòng mán bù。
He is walking amidst the snow.

他妨碍我把工作做好。
tā fáng ài wǒ bǎ gōng zuò zuò hào。
He impedes me to do the job well.

他对我的成功满怀羡慕。
tā duì wǒ de chéng gōng mǎn huái xiàn mù。
He was filled with envy at my success.

他对旅行作了十分生动的叙述。
tā duì lu:3 xíng zuò le shí fēn shēng dòng de xù shù。
He told a very descriptive account of his journey.

他对疯狂英语很着迷。
tā duì fēng kuáng Yīng yǔ hěn zháo mí。
He is crazy about Crazy English.

他对那个罪犯做出了裁决。
tā duì nèi gè zuì fàn zuò chū le cái jué。
He passed judgement on the guilty man.

他将作为伟大的政治家而载入史册。
tā jiàng zuò wéi wěi dà de zhèng zhì jiā ér zǎi rù shǐ cè。
He will go down in history as a great statesman.

他并没有把这首诗的意义真正揭示出来.
tā bìng méi yǒu bǎ zhè shǒu shī de yì yì zhēn zhèng jiē shì chū lai.
The meaning of the poem doesn't really come out in his interpretation.

他开始对工作感到厌倦。
tā kāi shǐ duì gōng zuò gǎn dào yàn juàn。
He began to weary of the work.

他总是叹息研究经费不足。
tā zǒng shì tàn xí yán jiū jīng fèi bù zú。
He always bemoans the shortage of funds for research.

他打算把财产转让给儿子。
tā dǎ suàn bǎ cái chǎn zhuǎn ràng jǐ ér zi。
He intends to transfer the property to his son.

他把椅子从窗户中抛出。
tā bǎ yǐ zi zòng chuāng hu zhòng pāo chū。
He hove a chair through the window.

他拐弯抹角地说她缺乏经验。
tā guǎi wān mò jué de shuō tā quē fá jīng yàn。
He made oblique references to her lack of experience.

他挤进两人中间，阻止他们打架。
tā jǐ jìn liǎng rén zhōng jiān， zǔ zhǐ tā men dǎ jià。
He interposed himself between them to stop them fighting.

他擦去铅笔的痕迹。
tā cā qù qiān bǐ de hén jī。
He erases pencil marks.

他是农村一大牧区的牧师.
tā shì nóng cūn yī dà mù qū de mù shī.
He is vicar of a large rural parish.

他是那么聪明，使我自愧不如。
tā shì nà me cōng míng， shǐ wǒ zì kuì bù rú。
He's so clever, he makes me feel inferior.

他最近去世给家庭聚会蒙上了阴影。
tā zuì jìn qù shì jǐ jiā tíng jù huì měng shàng le yīn yǐng。
His recent death overshadowed the family gathering.

他有个主意，以纯白为背景给他们拍摄。
tā yǒu gè zhǔ yi， yǐ chún bái wèi bèi jǐng jǐ tā men pāi shè。
He had the idea of shooting them against a complete plain white background.

他有才干能在本行业中首屈一指。
tā yǒu cái gàn néng zài běn háng yè zhòng shǒu qū yī zhǐ。
His ability carried him to the top of his profession.

他有权威，但并不想控制别人。
tā yǒu quán wēi， dàn bìng bù xiǎng kòng zhì bié rén。
He has authority, but he doesn't try to dominate others.

他欣然接受了我的报价。
tā xīn rán jiē shòu le wǒ de bào jià。
He pounced on my offer.

他渴望拥有权力。
tā kě wàng yōng yǒu quán lì。
He was thirsty for power.

他点燃了生日蛋糕上的小蜡烛。
tā diǎn rán le shēng rì dàn gāo shàng de xiǎo là zhú。
He lit the candles on the birthday cake.

他用蒸汽把信封上的邮票揭下来。
tā yòng zhēng qì bǎ xìn fēng shàng de yóu piào jiē xia lai。
He steamed the stamp off the envelope.

他申请出国签证经历了很大的困难。
tā shēn qǐng chū guó qiān zhèng jīng lì le hěn dà de kùn nan。
He experienced great difficulty in getting a visa to leave the country.

他病了很久，因此耽误了功课。
tā bìng le hěn jiǔ， yīn cǐ dān wu le gōng kè。
He had been ill for a long time and consequently he was behind in his work.

他的关于种族隔离的谈话激起了骚动。
tā de guān yú zhǒng zú gé lí de tán huà jī qǐ le sāo dòng。
His talk about apartheid created agitation.

他的态度既冷淡又无动于衷。
tā de tài du jì lěng dàn yòu wú dòng yú zhōng。
His manner was cold and indifferent.

他的死使我们大家都大为震惊。
tā de sǐ shǐ wǒ men dà jiā dōu dà wèi zhèn jīng。
His death was a great shock to us all.

他的画在画廊展出。
tā de huà zài huà láng zhǎn chū。
His pictures were showed in the gallery.

他的经验缓慢地成熟。
tā de jīng yàn huǎn màn de chéng shú。
His experience has a slow maturity.

他穿着一条沾满油污的旧牛仔裤。
tā chuān zhuó yī tiáo zhān mǎn yóu wū de jiù niú zǎi kù。
He wears an oily old pair of jeans.

他给后世留下了不朽的典范。
tā jǐ hòu shì liú xià le bù xiǔ de diǎn fàn。
He left behind an immortal example to all posterity.

他表示了振振有词的抗议。
tā biǎo shì le zhèn zhèn yǒu cí de kàng yì。
He expressed voluble protests.

他被一头野猪袭击。
tā bèi yī tóu yě zhū xí jī。
He was attacked by a wild boar.

他被他的老板解雇了。
tā bèi tā de lǎo bǎn jiě gù le。
He was fired by his boss.

他被家庭束缚，不能再到处去旅游了。
tā bèi jiā tíng shù fù， bù néng zài dào chù qù lu:3 yóu le。
He was fettered by his family and could not travel any longer.

他被罚款200美元。
tā bèi fá kuǎn200 měi yuán。
He was fined 200 dollars.

他过去的经历笼罩着神秘气氛。
tā guò qu de jīng lì lǒng zhào zhuó shén mì qì fēn。
His past is enveloped in a shroud of mystery.

他靠辛勤劳动而获得成功.
tā kào xīn qín láo dòng ér huò dé chéng gōng.
His success was achieved by hard work.

以音乐和舞蹈庆祝他的胜利。
yǐ yīn yuè huò wǔ dǎo qìng zhù tā de shèng lì。
His victory was celebrated with music and dancing.

你妈妈是个乐呵呵的容易相处的人。
nǐ mā ma shì gè yuè hē hē de róng yì xiāng chǔ de rén。
Your mother is a jolly, easy-going woman.

你若对我们的报价感兴趣，请与我们联系。
nǐ ruò duì wǒ men de bào jià gǎn xìng qu， qǐng yù wǒ men lián xì。
Should you be interested in our offer, please contact us.

你走时别忘了锁门。
nǐ zǒu shí biè wàng le suǒ mén。
Don't neglect to lock the door when you leave.

偶然的相遇使两位老朋友重新聚首。
ǒu rán de xiāng yù shǐ liǎng wèi lǎo péng you chóng xīn jù shǒu。
A chance meeting brought the two old friends together again.

全镇沉浸在节日的气氛之中。
quán zhèn chén jìn zài jié rì de qì fēn zhī zhōng。
The whole town is in a festive mood.

别忘了仔细记下你的开支帐目。
biè wàng le zǐ xì jì xià nǐ de kāi zhī zhàng mù。
Don't forget to keep a careful tally of what you spend.

别把热水倒进玻璃杯里，不然它会炸的。
biè bǎ rè shuǐ dào jìn bō li bēi lǐ， bù rán tā kuài zhà de。
Don't pour hot water into the glass or it will crack.

别那么敏感，我不是在批评你。
biè nà me mǐn gǎn， wǒ bú shì zài pī píng nǐ。
Don't be so sensitive - I was not criticizing you.

勉强他做事不是教育孩子的办法。
miǎn qiǎng tā zuò shì bú shì jiào yù hái zi de bàn fǎ。
It is not the way to educate a child by making him do things against his will.

历史常为偏见所曲解。
lì shǐ cháng wèi piān jiàn suǒ qǔ xiè。
Histories are often warped by biases.

去年这个镇已有十起破产事件。
qù nián zhè gè zhèn yǐ yǒu shí qǐ pò chǎn shì jiàn。
Ten bankruptcies were recorded in this town last year.

发展的主要障碍是这个国家人口太多。
fā zhǎn de zhǔ yào zhàng ài shì zhè gè guó jiā rén kǒu tài duō。
The main impediment to development is the country's large population.

只留下一些被太阳晒得泛白的枯骨。
zhǐ liú xià yī xiē bèi tài yáng shài de fàn bái de kū gǔ。
There were only a few dry bones left, bleached by the sun.

史密斯先生在政府的行政部门工作。
shǐ mì sī xiān sheng zài zhèng fǔ de xíng zhèng bù mén gōng zuò。
Mr. Smith works in an executive branch of the government.

史密斯夫人教那些快五岁的儿童。
shǐ mì sī fū ren jiào nà xiē kuài wǔ suì de ér tóng。
Mrs Smith teaches the rising fives.

史密斯教授曾做过总统的特别顾问。
shǐ mì sī jiào shòu zēng zuò guò zǒng tǒng de tè bié gù wèn。
Professor Smith served as special adviser to the President.

向公司索取退款手续很复杂。
xiàng gōng sī suǒ qǔ tuì kuǎn shǒu xù hěn fù zá。
Obtaining a refund from the company is a complicated procedure.

听到朋友死亡的消息，她难过地哭了。
tīng dào péng you sǐ wáng de xiāo xi， tā nán guò de kū le。
She cried with grief when she heard news of her friend's death.

听到这个坏消息，他心里充满恐怖。
tīng dào zhè gè huài xiāo xi， tā xīn lǐ chōng mǎn kǒng bù。
He was filled with horror at the bad news.

听到这个消息，他惊讶得张口结舌。
tīng dào zhè gè xiāo xi， tā jīng yà de zhāng kǒu jié shé。
On hearing the news, his jaw dropped.

听音乐对她起了一种镇静的作用。
tìng yīn yuè duì tā qǐ le yī zhòng zhèn jìng de zuò yòng。
Listening to the music has a calming influence on her.

吵闹声使他烦躁。
chǎo nào shēng shǐ tā fán zào。
The loud noise chafed him.

咱们来把它们用胶水粘在一块儿。
zán men lái bǎ tā men yòng jiāo shuǐ zhān zài yī kuài er。
Let's stick them together with gum.

咱们索性把蛋糕吃完吧, 也没剩多少了.
zán men suǒ xìng bǎ dàn gāo chī wán ba,  yě mò shèng duō shao le.
We might as well finish (up) the cake; there isn't much left.

哦，也许我错了。
ó， yě xǔ wǒ cuò le。
Oh, maybe I was wrong.

哨兵查问在门口的陌生人.
shào bīng zhā wèn zài mén kǒu de mò shēng rén.
The sentry challenged the stranger at the gates.

圣诞节是基督教徒的一个重要节日。
Shèng dàn jié shì Jī dū jiào tú de yī gè zhòng yào jié rì。
Christmas is an important feast for Christians.

圣诞节是基督教的节日。
Shèng dàn jié shì Jī dū jiào de jié rì。
Christmas is a festival of the Christian Church.

在新政权下，事情将会发生变化。
zài xīn zhèng quán xià， shì qing jiāng huì fā shēng biàn huà。
Things will change under the new regime.

在日本，棒球比其他任何运动都受人欢迎。
zài Rì běn， bàng qiú bì qí tā rèn hé yùn dòng dōu shòu rén huān yíng。
Baseball is more popular than any other sport in Japan.

在英国，车辆必须靠左行驶。
zài Yīng guó， chē liàng bì xū kào zuǒ xíng shǐ。
In England traffic must keep to the left.

在这个陌生的地方，我觉得很不自在。
zài zhè gè mò shēng de dì fang， wǒ jué de hěn bù zì zài。
I don't feel at ease in the strange place.

在这场足球赛中，他主罚，踢进了一个球。
zài zhè chǎng zú qiú sài zhòng， tā zhǔ fá， tī jìn le yī gè qiú。
He kicked a penalty goal in the football match.

在这座陌生的城市里，她感到很寂寞。
zài zhè zuò mò shēng de chéng shì lǐ， tā gǎn dào hěn jì mò。
She feels rather lonely in the strange town.

在重要的节日, 人们把国旗悬挂在门外。
zài zhòng yào de jié rì,  rén men bǎ guó qí xuán guà zài mén wài。
People hang national flags out on important holidays.

基督派基督十二使徒之一宣传他的教义。
Jī dū pài Jī dū shí èr shǐ tú zhī yī xuān chuán tā de jiào yì。
Apostles were sent out by Christ to spread his teachings.

大群人聚集在展览大厅的门口。
dà qún rén jù jí zài zhǎn lǎn dà tīng de mén kǒu。
A multitude of people gathered at the gate of the exhibition hall.

大雪妨碍了这项建筑工程的进行。
dà xuě fáng ài le zhè xiàng jiàn zhù gōng chéng de jìn xíng。
Heavy snow hindered the construction work.

天黑了，我把窗帘拉上。
tiān hēi le， wǒ bǎ chuāng lián lā shàng。
I drew the curtain as it was getting dark.

女朋友最喜欢的女性同伴或爱人
nu:3 péng you zuì xǐ huan de nu:3 xìng tóng bàn huò ài ren
A favored female companion or sweetheart.

她一辈子搞戏剧。
tā yī bèi zi gǎo xì jù。
She is been in the theater all her life.

她匆匆赶往机场。
tā cōng cōng gǎn wàng jī chǎng。
She hurried to the airport.

她只有坐在壁炉前才感觉到暖和。
tā zhǐ yǒu zuò zài bì lú qián cái gǎn jué dào nuǎn huó。
She felt warm only when she sat before the fireplace.

她太倒霉了，休假第一天就感冒了。
tā tài dǎo méi le， xiū jià dì yī tiān jiù gǎn mào le。
She was unlucky to catch a cold on the first day of her holiday.

她太小了，不能骑脚踏车。
tā tài xiǎo le， bù néng qí jué tà jū。
She is too little to ride a bicycle.

她如饥似渴地收集一切有关的信息。
tā rú jī sì kě de shōu jí yī qiè yǒu guān de xìn xī。
She gobbled up all the relevant information.

她对计算机有广博的知识。
tā duì jì suàn jī yǒu guǎng bó de zhī shi。
She has a broad knowledge of computers.

她所有的钱都投放到股票里去了。
tā suǒ yǒu de qián dōu tóu fàng dào gǔ piào lǐ qù le。
She's got all her money in stocks and shares.

她打开卧室的门走了进去.
tā dǎ kāi wò shì de mén zǒu le jìn qù.
She opened the bedroom door and went in.

她把孩子抱在怀里.
tā bǎ hái zi bào zài huái lǐ.
She nestled the baby in her arms.

她把糖搅和到咖啡里。
tā bǎ táng jiǎo huò dào kā fēi lǐ。
She stirred the sugar into her coffee.

她挣扎著想摆脱那个侵犯她的人.
tā zhēng zhá著 xiǎng bǎi tuō nèi gè qīn fàn tā de rén.
She struggled to get away from her attacker.

她是一名公共汽车售票员。
tā shì yī míng gōng gòng qì chē shòu piào yuán。
She is a bus conductor.

她渴望摆脱母亲的操纵.
tā kě wàng bǎi tuō mǔ qīn de cāo zòng.
She longed to escape from her mother's domination.

她的命运一直与悲哀相连。
tā de mìng yùn yī zhí yù bēi āi xiāng lián。
Sorrow has always been her portion.

她的美貌倾倒了很多男青年。
tā de měi mào qīng dào le hěn duō nán qīng nián。
Her beauty enslaved many young men.

她讲了一辈子中文。
tā jiǎng le yī bèi zi Zhōng wén。
She has spoken Chinese all her life.

如果你再迟到，你将被解雇。
rú guǒ nǐ zài chí dào， nǐ jiàng bèi jiě gù。
If you are late again, you will be dismissed.

如果你再迟到，老板就会把你解雇。
rú guǒ nǐ zài chí dào， lǎo bǎn jiù kuài bǎ nǐ jiě gù。
If you are late again the boss will give you the sack.

如果机器出故障，就把开关关掉。
rú guǒ jī qì chū gù zhàng， jiù bǎ kāi guān guān diào。
Turn off the switch when anything goes wrong with the machine.

宇宙飞船正绕月球飞行。
yǔ zhòu fēi chuán zhèng rào yuè qiú fēi xíng。
The spacecraft is orbiting the moon.

将军推测说敌人将于今天晚上突袭我们。
jiāng jūn tuī cè shuō dí rén jiàng yú jīn tiān wǎn shang tū xí wǒ men。
The general conjectures that the enemy will launch an attack against us this night.

小女孩在河里淹死了。
xiǎo nu:3 hái zài hé lǐ yān sǐ le。
The little girl drowned in the river.

小孩有柔软的身体。
xiǎo hái yǒu róu ruǎn de shēn tǐ。
Little babies have lithe bodies.

峡谷常常有河流经过其中。
xiá gǔ cháng cháng yǒu hé liú jīng guò qí zhōng。
A canyon usually has a river flowing through it.

工会为争取更好的工作条件而罢工。
gōng huì wèi zhēng qǔ gèng hǎo de gōng zuò tiáo jiàn ér bà gōng。
The union struck for better work conditions.

希尔先生和夫人招待客人真周到.
xī ěr xiān sheng huò fū ren zhāo dài kè ren zhēn zhōu dào.
Mr and Mrs Hill are such good hosts.

幸福和财富不能混为一谈。
xìng fú huò cái fù bù néng hùn wèi yī tán。
One can not identify happiness with wealth.

床头上有一个长枕垫。
chuáng tou shàng yǒu yī gè zhǎng zhěn diàn。
There is a bolster across the head of the bed.

建议肥胖病人改变饮食.
jiàn yì féi pán bìng rén gǎi biàn yǐn shí.
Obese patients are advised to change their diet.

很多种类的动物现在已经从地球上绝迹了。
hěn duō zhǒng lèi de dòng wù xiàn zài yǐ jīng zòng dì qiú shàng jué jī le。
Many types of animals have now vanished from the earth.

很遗憾，你没有得到那份工作。
hěn yí hàn， nǐ méi yǒu dé dào nà fèn gōng zuò。
I'm sorry that you didn't get the job.

想在这样大的暴风雪中去爬山简直是疯狂。
xiǎng zài zhè yàng dà de bào fēng xuě zhòng qù pá shān jiǎn zhí shì fēng kuáng。
It would be madness to try to climb the mountain in such a snowstorm.

我上个月瘦了好几磅。
wǒ shàng gè yuè shòu le hǎo jǐ bàng。
I lost several pounds last month.

我不喜欢喝速溶咖啡。
wǒ bù xǐ huan hè sù róng kā fēi。
I don't like to drink instant coffee.

我不愿意在交通高峰时间出去。
wǒ bù yuàn yì zài jiāo tōng gāo fēng shí jiān chū qù。
I don't like to go out during the rush hour.

我与其嫁给他，倒不如去死算了。
wǒ yǔ qí jià jǐ tā， dào bù rú qù sǐ suàn le。
I may as well die as marry him.

我了解一些世界上的神秘宗教。
wǒ liǎo jiě yī xiē shì jiè shàng de shén mì zōng jiào。
I know some world's mystic religions.

我以零售方式买来这些牛奶。
wǒ yǐ líng shòu fāng shì mǎi lái zhè xie niú nǎi。
I bought the milk retail.

我们从悬崖顶上的高处能看到城市的全景。
wǒ men zòng xuán yá dǐng shàng de gāo chù néng kàn dào chéng shì de quán jǐng。
From our perch up there on top of the cliff we can see the whole town.

我们会把决定及早通知申请者。
wǒ men kuài bǎ jué dìng jí zǎo tōng zhī shēn qǐng zhě。
Applicants will be notified of our decision in good season.

我们喜欢观赏初升太阳的灿烂光辉。
wǒ men xǐ huan guān shǎng chū shēng tài yáng de càn làn guāng huī。
We enjoy seeing the glorious beams of the rising sun.

我们在黑暗中摸索。
wǒ men zài hēi àn zhòng mō suo。
We groped amid the darkness.

我们宁死而不投降。
wǒ men níng sǐ ér bù tóu xiáng。
We would rather die than surrender.

我们已经收到了对该节目的一连串投诉。
wǒ men yǐ jīng shōu dào le duì gāi jié mù de yī lián chuàn tóu sù。
We have had a string of complaints about the program.

我们忠于祖国。
wǒ men zhōng yú zǔ guó。
We are loyal to our motherland.

我们摸索着走过黑暗的街道。
wǒ men mō suo zhuó zǒu guò hēi àn de jiē dào。
We groped our way through the dark streets.

我们明天必须离开，真是遗憾。
wǒ men míng tiān bì xū lí kāi， zhēn shì yí hàn。
It is a pity that we shall have to leave tomorrow.

我们昨晚畅饮了一次酒。
wǒ men zuó wǎn chàng yǐn le yī cì jiǔ。
We quaffed wine last night.

我们有可能从这片浅滩过河。
wǒ men yǒu kě néng zòng zhè piàn qiǎn tān guò hé。
This shallow ford made it possible for us to cross the river.

我们点燃了蜡烛，蜡烛照亮了房间。
wǒ men diǎn rán le là zhú， là zhú zhào liàng le fáng jiān。
We lit the candle and the candle lit the room.

我们经济的决定性因素是控制通货膨胀。
wǒ men jīng jì de jué dìng xìng yīn sù shì kòng zhì tōng huò péng zhàng。
The determinate factor of our economy is to control inflation.

我们能用半径计算出圆的面积。
wǒ men néng yòng bàn jìng jì suàn chū yuán de miàn ji。
We can compute the circular area with radius.

我们走时车子扬起了一阵尘土。
wǒ men zǒu shí jū zi yáng qǐ le yī zhèn chén tǔ。
The car raised quite a dust as we drove off.

我们送些酬劳，对您的大力协助聊表谢意。
wǒ men sòng xiē chóu láo， duì nín de dà lì xié zhù liáo biǎo xiè yì。
We are sending you some money in acknowledgement of your valuable help.

我们都喜欢乡村生活的宁静。
wǒ men dōu xǐ huan xiāng cūn shēng huó de níng jìng。
We all like the tranquility of the country life.

我倾向于相信他的无辜。
wǒ qīng xiàng yú xiāng xìn tā de wú gū。
I'm inclined to believe him innocent.

我冒雨出去，结果被淋得湿透了。
wǒ mào yǔ chū qù， jié guǒ bèi lìn de shī tòu le。
I went out in the rain and got wet through.

我刚才把你的一个瓷器装饰品弄掉了。
wǒ gāng cái bǎ nǐ de yī gè cí qì zhuāng shì pǐn nòng diào le。
I've just dropped one of your china ornamental.

我只耽搁你几分钟。
wǒ zhǐ dān ge nǐ jǐ fēn zhōng。
I'll only keep you a few minutes.

我喜欢戴银首饰。
wǒ xǐ huan dài yín shǒu shì。
I like to wear argentine jewellery.

我喜欢熟桃的香甜味。
wǒ xǐ huan shú táo de xiāng tián wèi。
I like the luscious taste of ripe peaches.

我在卧室里发现两只袜子, 但不成对。
wǒ zài wò shì lǐ fā xiàn liǎng zhǐ wà zi,  dàn bù chéng duì。
I found a couple of socks in the bedroom, but they don't make a pair.

我在夏天一个闷热的下午遇见了她。
wǒ zài xià tiān yī gè mēn rè de xià wǔ yù jiàn le tā。
I met her in a sultry summer afternoon.

我在街道对面的连锁商店里买了这只面包。
wǒ zài jiē dào duì miàn de lián suǒ shāng diàn lǐ mǎi le zhè zhǐ miàn bāo。
I bought this loaf of bread in the chain store opposite the street.

我希望他成为钢琴家的梦想可以成真。
wǒ xī wàng tā chéng wéi gāng qín jiā de mèng xiǎng kě yǐ chéng zhēn。
I hope his dream of becoming a pianist will come true.

我把赚的钱都花光了。
wǒ bǎ zuàn de qián dōu huā guāng le。
I've spent all my earnings.

我把钥匙掉在这附近某个地方了。
wǒ bǎ yào shi diào zài zhè fù jìn mǒu gè dì fang le。
I dropped my key somewhere about here.

我挣多少钱与你无关。
wǒ zhèng duō shao qián yù nǐ wú guān。
How much money I earn is none of your concern.

我昨晚喝了一小瓶白兰地。
wǒ zuó wǎn hè le yī xiǎo píng bái lán de。
I drank a miniature bottle of brandy last night.

我是在教堂的门廊处遇到那个人的。
wǒ shì zài jiào táng de mén láng chù yù dào nèi gè rén de。
I met that person at the porch of the church.

我有一件红色的华达呢上衣。
wǒ yǒu yī jiàn hóng sè de huà dá ne shàng yī。
I have a red gabardine coat.

我每天早晨吃一碗麦片粥。
wǒ měi tiān zǎo chén jí yī wǎn mài piàn zhōu。
I have a bowl of cereal every morning.

我浑身疼痛。
wǒ hún shēn téng tòng。
I ache all over.

我疯狂地渴望去完成那件事。
wǒ fēng kuáng de kě wàng qù wán chéng nà jiàn shì。
I have an insane desire to finish that thing.

我的弟弟是饲养牛的饲养员。
wǒ de dì di shì sì yǎng niú de sì yǎng yuán。
My brother is a cattle breeder.

我相信她照顾孤儿是件好事。
wǒ xiāng xìn tā zhào gu gū ér shì jiàn hǎo shì。
I believe it good her taking care of orphans.

我离开巴黎已经两星期了。
wǒ lí kāi Bā lí yǐ jīng liǎng xīng qī le。
I have been away from Paris for two weeks.

我若还清所有欠债就分文不剩了.
wǒ ruò huán qīng suǒ yǒu qiàn zhài jiù fèn wén bù shèng le.
If I pay all my debts I'll have no money left.

我见希尔夫人面熟, 但并不相识.
wǒ xiàn xī ěr fū ren miàn shú,  dàn bìng bù xiāng shí.
I know Mrs Hill by sight, but we've never met.

我认为我和我女儿之间没有隔阂。
wǒ rèn wéi wǒ huò wǒ nu:3 ér zhī jiān méi yǒu gé hé。
I think there is no gulf between my daughter and I.

我请求他从新疆回来时给我带些葡萄干。
wǒ qǐng qiú tā zòng xīn jiāng huí lai shí jǐ wǒ dài xiē pú tao gàn。
I asked him to bring me some raisins when he returns from Xinjiang.

我送给她一条编织的披肩作圣诞礼物。
wǒ sòng jǐ tā yī tiáo biān zhī de pī jiān zuò Shèng dàn lǐ wù。
I gave her a knitted shawl as a Christmas gift.

我钱很宽裕，能帮助她。
wǒ qián hěn kuān yù， néng bāng zhù tā。
As I had plenty of money I was able to help her.

所有的申请者一个接着一个参加面试。
suǒ yǒu de shēn qǐng zhě yī gè jiē zhe yī gè cān jiā miàn shì。
All the applicants were interviewed one by one.

所有的窗户都用砖堵住了。
suǒ yǒu de chuāng hu dōu yòng zhuān dǔ zhù le。
All the windows were bricked up.

打完电话后，请把听筒放回原位。
dǎ wán diàn huà hòu， qǐng bǎ tìng tǒng fàng huí yuán wèi。

拍照时照相机不要晃.

据说法国人是世界上最浪漫的民族之一。
jù shuō fǎ guó rén shì shì jiè shàng zuì làng màn de mín zú zhī yī。
It is said that Frenchmen are among the most romantic people in the world.

政府力图在这个问题上保持低姿态。
zhèng fǔ lì tú zài zhè gè wèn tí shàng bǎo chí dī zī tài。
The government is trying to keep a low profile on this issue.

政府将派军驻守沿海的城镇。
zhèng fǔ jiàng pài jūn zhù shǒu yán hǎi de chéng zhèn。

政治和宗教是人们平常交谈的主要话题。
zhèng zhì huò zōng jiào shì rén men píng cháng jiāo tán de zhǔ yào huà tí。
Politics and religion are daily topics of conversation.

教士那圆润低沉的声音在教堂里回响。
jiào shì nà yuán rùn dī chén de shēng yīn zài jiào táng lǐ huí xiǎng。
The sonorous voice of the priest resounded in the church.

整顿饭都很好, 尤其是葡萄酒更好.
zhěng dùn fàn dōu hěn hǎo,  yóu qí shì pú tao jiǔ gèng hǎo.
The whole meal was good but the wine in particular was excellent.

新的税收制度将于明年实行。
xīn de shuì shōu zhì dù jiàng yú míng nián shí xíng。
A new system of taxation will be brought into effect next year.

无轨电车的电能是通过架空线供给的。
wú guǐ diàn chē de diàn néng shì tōng guò jià kòng xiàn gōng gěi de。

春天里万物欣欣向荣。
chūn tiān lǐ wàn wù xīn xīn xiàng róng。

昨天的这个时候正刮着狂风。
zuó tiān de zhè gè shí hou zhèng guā zhuó kuáng fēng。
It was blowing gales of hurricane this time yesterday.

智能并不像品性那样有影响。
zhì néng bìng bù xiàng pǐn xìng nà yàng yǒu yǐng xiǎng。
It is not intellect that tells so much as character.

暴风给成千上万的人带来灾难。
bào fēng jǐ chéng qiān shàng wàn de rén dài lái zāi nàn。
The cyclone brought misery to thousands of people.

暴风雨时，我正在树下躲避。
bào fēng yǔ shí， wǒ zhèng zài shù xià duǒ bì。

暴风雨来临时，天空转暗。
bào fēng yǔ lái lín shí， tiān kōng zhuàn àn。
The sky turned dark as the storm came near.

有些罪犯被释放后有可能重新犯罪。
yǒu xiē zuì fàn bèi shì fàng hòu yǒu kě néng chóng xīn fàn zuì。
Some criminals are likely to offend again when they are released.

有炸鸡肉作晚餐。
yǒu zhà jī ròu zuò wǎn cān。
There was fried chicken for dinner.

根据解剖结果，此人死于心脏病发作。
gēn jù jiě pōu jié guǒ， cǐ rén sǐ yú xīn zàng bìng fā zuò。

植物因缺水而枯死了。
zhí wù yīn quē shuǐ ér kū sǐ le。

殖民地的人们拿起武器反抗英国统治者。
zhí mín dì de rén men ná qǐ wǔ qì fǎn kàng Yīng guó tǒng zhì zhē。
The colonists took up weapons to rebel against the British ruler.

每周六琴在村里的公用草地上骑马。
měi zhōu liù qín zài cūn lǐ de gōng yòng cǎo dì shàng qí mǎ。
Every Saturday Jean went riding on the village common.

每年春天河水把山谷淹没。
měi nián chūn tiān hé shuǐ bǎ shān gǔ yān mò。
Every spring the river floods the valley.

汽车停止时震动了一下。
qì chē tíng zhǐ shí zhèn dòng le yī xià。
The car stopped with a jolt.

汽车和电车塞满了整条街。
qì chē huò diàn chē sè mǎn le zhěng tiáo jiē。

法官判他罚款10 美元。
fǎ guān pàn tā fá kuǎn10  měi yuán。

海关人员问我是否有要报税的东西。
hǎi guān rén yuán wèn wǒ shì fǒu yǒu yào bào shuì de dōng xi。
The customs asked me if I had anything to declare.

混凝土墙是用钢筋加固的。
hùn níng tǔ qiáng shì yòng gāng jīn jiā gù de。
The concrete walls are reinforced with steel rods.

湿润的风从南方吹来。
shī rùn de fēng zòng nán fāng chuī lái。

满是尘土的路弄得行人也满面尘土了。

炮兵部署在西边.
pào bīng bù shǔ zài xī biān.

zhè tiáo lù bǎ suǒ yǒu de xīn chéng zhèn dōu lián jiē qǐ lai le。
The road links all the new towns.

这样浪费金钱简直是罪恶。
zhè yàng làng fèi jīn qián jiǎn zhí shì zuì è。
It's a wicked waste of money.

这次地震是个可怕的灾难。
zhè cì dì zhèn shì gè kě pà de zāi nàn。
The earthquake was a terrible catastrophe.

这次聚会单调乏味。
zhè cì jù huì dān diào fá wèi。
The party was a dull affair.

这种建筑风格让我感到很压抑。
zhè zhǒng jiàn zhù fēng gé ràng wǒ gǎn dào hěn yā yì。
This kind of architectural style depresses me.

这种物质能够溶解在酒精中。
zhè zhǒng wù zhì néng gòu róng jiě zài jiǔ jīng zhòng。
This substance is soluble in alcohol.

这管子柔软但很坚固。
zhè guǎn zi róu ruǎn dàn hěn jiān gù。
This tube is flexible but tough.

这艘船被敌人的鱼雷击沉了。
zhè sōu chuán bèi dí rén de yú léi jī chén le。
The ship was sunk by an enemy torpedo.

这辆卡车最大载重量是一吨。
zhè liàng kǎ chē zuì dà zài zhòng liàng shì yī dùn。
The maximum load for this lorry is one ton.

这部小说里的叙述比对话多.
zhè bù xiǎo shuō lǐ de xù shù bì duì huà duō.
The novel contains more narrative than dialogue.

这间屋子陈设得简单朴素。
zhè jiàn wū zi chén shè de jiǎn dān pǔ sù。
The room was furnished in austere style.

进口食品可赚钱。
jìn kǒu shí pǐn kě zhuàn qián。
It is profitable to import food.

选择权已不在他们手中了。
xuǎn zé quán yǐ bù zài tā men shǒu zhòng le。
The choice is no longer in their disposition.

造成死亡的直接原因不明.
zào chéng sǐ wáng de zhí jiē yuán yīn bù míng.
The immediate cause of death is unknown.

那个口琴质量很好。
nèi gè kǒu qín zhì liàng hěn hǎo。
The harmonica is of very high quality.

那个抄写员辛勤工作来养家。
nèi gè chāo xiě yuán xīn qín gōng zuò lái yǎng jiā。
The scribe worked hard to support his family.

那个男人曾是个好色之徒。
nèi gè nán rén zēng shì gè hào shǎi zhī tú。
That man used to be a lascivious person.

那个邮递员被一只恶狗咬了。
nèi gè yóu dì yuán bèi yī zhǐ wù gǒu yǎo le。
The postman was bitten by a fierce dog.

那些战士都裹着绑腿。
nà xiē zhàn shì dōu guǒ zhuó bǎng tuǐ。
Those soldiers all wear leggings.

那儿有很多喂牛的饲料。
nà r yǒu hěn duō wèi niú de sì liào。
There is much forage for the cattle.

那块石头差点儿砸到男孩。
nà kuài shí tou cī diǎn er zá dào nán hái。
The stone just missed the boy.

那条街经常交通阻塞。
nà tiáo jiē jīng cháng jiāo tōng zǔ sè。
There is always traffic congestion in that street.

那条路是用鹅卵石铺成的。
nà tiáo lù shì yòng é luǎn shí pù chéng de。
The road was paved with cobblestones.

那次宴会上有大量饮料供应。
nà cì yàn huì shàng yǒu dà liàng yǐn liào gōng yìng。
There was a liberal supply of drinks at the party.

那狗一路跟在我身旁边喘边跑.
nà gǒu yī lù gēn zài wǒ shēn páng biān chuǎn biān pǎo.
The dog panted along (the road) beside me.

那老人好容易喘著气说出几句话。
nà lǎo rén hào róng yì chuǎn著 qì shuō chū jǐ jù huà。
The old man manage to puff out a few words.

那顶帽子上饰有彩色珠子。
nà dǐng mào zi shàng shì yǒu cǎi sè zhū zi。
The hat was decorated with colored beads.

酬金将与工作量成比例.
chóu jīn jiàng yù gōng zuò liàng chéng bǐ lì.
Payment will be proportional to the amount of work done.

酸与碱反应生成盐。
suān yù jiǎn fǎn yìng shēng chéng yán。
Acids react with bases to form salts.

酸把银器的表面腐蚀了。
suān bǎ yín qì de biǎo miàn fǔ shí le。
Acid had pitted the surface of the silver.

钢笔从我指缝中滑下去了。
gāng bǐ zòng wǒ zhǐ fèng zhòng huá xià qu le。
The pen slips out of my fingers.

钥匙都在接待处呢.
yào shi dōu zài jiē dài chù ne.
The keys are with reception.

铁容易生锈。
tiě róng yì shēng xiù。
Iron is apt to rust.

铁很容易氧化。
tiě hěn róng yì yǎng huà。
Iron is easily oxidized.

镇外有个垃圾场。
zhèn wài yǒu gè垃圾 chǎng。
There is a refuse dump out of the town.

门稍微开了条缝。
mén shāo wēi kāi le tiáo fèng。
The door opened a fraction.

阳光透过窗帘映了进来。
yáng guāng tòu guò chuāng lián yìng le jìn lái。
The sunlight filtered through the curtains.

随便摘花的人会被罚款。
suí biàn zhāi huā de rén kuài bèi fá kuǎn。
They will impose a fine on anyone who should pick flowers at will.

隔壁房间里突然爆发出一阵笑声。
gé bì fáng jiān lǐ tū rán bào fā chū yī zhèn xiào shēng。
There was a burst of laughter in the next room.

饥荒往往是战争或干旱造成的。
jī huang wǎng wǎng shì zhàn zhēng huò gān hàn zào chéng de。
Famine is often the sequel to war or drought.

饥饿引起犯罪。
jī è yǐn qǐ fàn zuì。
Hunger begets crime.

饥饿的狮子撕碎了猎物。
jī è de shī zi sī suì le liè wù。
The ravenous lion tore the quarry.

饲养员正在喂动物。
sì yǎng yuán zhèng zài wèi dòng wù。
The keeper is feeding the animals.

鱼浮到水面上捕捉昆虫。
yú fú dào shuǐ miàn shàng bǔ zhuō kūn chóng。
Fish were surfacing to catch insects.

鸟在笼中拍著翅膀.
niǎo zài lóng zhòng pāi著 chì bǎng.
The bird fluttered its wings in the cage.

黑暗会使他更加珍惜视力。
hēi àn kuài shǐ tā gèng jiā zhēn xī shì lì。
Darkness would make him more appreciative of sight.

一个人未被证明有罪前，被视为是清白的。
yī gè rén wèi bèi zhèng míng yǒu zuì qián， bèi shì wéi shì qīng bái de。
A man is accounted innocent until he is proven guilty.

一支孤烛使黑暗的房间亮了起来。
yī zhī gū zhú shǐ hēi àn de fáng jiān liàng le qǐ lai。
A solitary candle lightened the darkness of the room.

一组护士协助医生施行手术。
yī zǔ hù shi xié zhù yī shēng shī xíng shǒu shù。
A team of nurses assisted the doctor in performing the operation.

下星期，他将要参加一场国际象棋比赛。
xià xīng qī， tā jiāng yào cān jiā yī chǎng guó jì xiàng qí bǐ sài。
He will take part in a chess tournament next week.

专业，主修课选作学术专业的一个研究领域
zhuān yè， zhǔ xiū kè xuǎn zuò xué shù zhuān yè de yī gè yán jiū lǐng yù
A field of study chosen as an academic specialty.

世代居住在城市里使他们磨练了才智。
shì dài jū zhù zài chéng shì lǐ shǐ tā men mò liàn le cái zhì。
Generations of urban living sharpened their wits.

个人清洁对于健康和仪表同样重要。
gè rén qīng jié duì yú jiàn kāng huò yí biǎo tóng yàng zhòng yào。
Personal cleanliness is important to health as well as to appearance.

主席的简短陈辞概括了委员会的观点.
zhǔ xí de jiǎn duǎn chén cí gài kuò le wěi yuán huì de guān diǎn.
The chairman's short statement encapsulates the views of the committee.

从右边驶来的车辆享有优先通行权.
zòng yòu biān shǐ lái de chē liàng xiǎng yǒu yōu xiān tōng xíng quán.
Vehicles coming from the right have priority.

从资料库借磁带是退而求其次的办法。
zòng zī liào kù jiè cí dài shì tuì ér qiú qí cì de bàn fǎ。
Borrowing tapes from the library would be the next-best thing.

他不听母亲的劝告，参加了那次聚会。
tā bù tìng mǔ qīn de quàn gào， cān jiā le nà cì jù huì。
He disobeyed his mother and went to the party.

他以两杆的成绩赢得了这场高尔夫球赛。
tā yǐ liǎng gǎn de chéng jī yíng dé le zhè chǎng gāo ěr fū qiú sài。
He won the golf match by two shots.

他们因对手权柄在握, 反抗也没用.
tā men yīn duì shǒu quán bǐng zài wò,  fǎn kàng yě méi yòng.
Their opponents had the whip hand and it was useless to resist.

他们是彼此争夺第一名的老对手。
tā men shì bǐ cǐ zhēng duó dì yī míng de lǎo duì shǒu。
They are old rivals vying with each other for first place.

他们沿着报春花盛开的河岸边走边聊。
tā men yán zhe bào chūn huā shèng kāi de hé àn biān zǒu biān liáo。
They walked along the primrose bank chatting.

他们钻透了几层岩石以寻找石油.
tā men zuàn tòu le jǐ céng yán shí yǐ xún zhǎo shí yóu.
They drilled through several layers of rock to reach the oil.

他偷偷溜进了电影院而没有被人逮着。
tā tōu tōu liū jìn le diàn yǐng yuàn ér méi yǒu bèi rén dài zhuó。
He stole into the cinema without being caught.

他公然蔑视上司，并要求他作出解释。
tā gōng rán miè shì shàng si， bìng yāo qiú tā zuò chū jiě shì。
He bearded his boss and demanded an explanation.

他出事后重新学习走路要有极大的毅力。
tā chū shì hòu chóng xīn xué xí zǒu lù yào yǒu jí dà de yì lì。
Learning to walk again after his accident required great patience.

他发出一声绝望的叹息，转身走开了。
tā fā chū yī shēng jué wàng de tàn xí， zhuǎn shēn zǒu kāi le。
With a hopeless sigh, he turned away.

他发挥艺术天才, 成了雕刻家.
tā fā huī yì shù tiān cái,  chéng le diāo kè jiā.
He turned his artistic gifts to good account by becoming a sculptor.

他叙述了他如何从13岁起就给人扛活。
tā xù shù le tā rú hé zò13ng suì qǐ jiù jǐ rén káng huó。
He related how he had worked as a farm-hand since he was thirteen.

他只是偶尔一次公开自己的观点。
tā zhǐ shì ǒu ěr yī cì gōng kāi zì jǐ de guān diǎn。
Only rarely does he let his own views become public.

他号召工人为争取自己的权利而斗争。
tā hào zhào gōng rén wèi zhēng qǔ zì jǐ de quán lì ér dòu zhēng。
He called on the workers to fight for their rights.

他因为玩忽职守而失去工作，罪有应得。
tā yīn wèi wàn hū zhí shǒu ér shī qù gōng zuò， zuì yǒu yīng dé。
It served him right to lose that job, because he neglected it.

他因遭蛇咬而被送到医院治疗。
tā yīn zāo shé yǎo ér bèi sòng dào yī yuàn zhì liáo。
He was taken to the hospital to be treated for snake bite.

他在股票交易中买卖精明, 赚了很多钱.
tā zài gǔ piào jiāo yì zhòng mǎi mài jīng míng,  zuàn le hěn duō qián.
His clever manipulation of the stock markets makes him lots of money.

他在青年时代曾经有过想当钢琴家的雄心。
tā zài qīng nián shí dài céng jīng yǒu guò xiǎng dàng gāng qín jiā de xióng xīn。
In his youth he had the ambition of being a pianist.

他很有礼貌地帮助那个老太太扛包裹。
tā hěn yǒu lǐ mào de bāng zhù nèi gè lǎo tài tai káng bāo guǒ。
It was courteous of him to help the old lady with her bundles.

他拣起信封时，一把钥匙掉了出来。
tā jiǎn qǐ xìn fēng shí， yī bǎ yào shi diào le chū lai。
As he picked up the envelope, a key dropped out.

他搜集以前的作品，编成了所谓的五经。
tā sōu jí yǐ qián de zuò pǐn， biān chéng le suǒ wèi de Wǔ Jīng。
He gathered earlier writings to prepare what are called the Five Classics.

他有才干能在本行业中首屈一指。
tā yǒu cái gàn néng zài běn háng yè zhòng shǒu qū yī zhǐ。
His ability carried him to the top of his profession.

他未做认真的调查就仓促做出了结论。
tā wèi zuò rèn zhēn de diào chá jiù cāng cù zuò chū le jié lùn。
He jumped to a conclusion without careful investigation.

他用冰凉的手捧起一杯滚热的巧克力饮料。
tā yòng bīng liáng de shǒu pěng qǐ yī bēi gǔn rè de qiǎo kè lì yǐn liào。
He cupped his cold hands round the cup of hot chocolate.

他用塑料铲把盆里的混合料刮了出来.
tā yòng sù liào chǎn bǎ pén lǐ de hùn hé liào guā le chū lai.
He scraped the mixture out of the bowl with a plastic spatula.

他的母亲已经把他训练成循规蹈矩的人。
tā de mǔ qīn yǐ jīng bǎ tā xùn liàn chéng xún guī dǎo jǔ de rén。
His mother has trained him to be a very proper young man.

他的话对社区所有成员是故意的侮辱。
tā de huà duì shè qū suǒ yǒu chéng yuán shì gù yì de wǔ rù。
His speech was an affront to all members of the community.

他的话已在他们心中播下怀疑的种子。
tā de huà yǐ zài tā men xīn zhōng bō xià huái yí de zhǒng zi。
His words had sowed the seeds of suspicion in their minds.

他站在边上等待跳水时浑身发抖.
tā zhàn zài biān shàng děng dài tiào shuǐ shí hún shēn fā dǒu.
He stood shivering on the brink, waiting to dive in.

他索赔过高反而使他的要求无法实现。
tā suǒ péi guò gāo fǎn ér shǐ tā de yāo qiú wú fǎ shí xiàn。
He prejudiced his claim by demanding too much compensation.

他终生献身于珍稀动物的保护。
tā zhōng shēng xiàn shēn yú zhēn xī dòng wù de bǎo hù。
He's devoted his whole life to the protection of the rare animals.

他舒展开身体躺在炉火旁边睡著了.
tā shū zhǎn kāi shēn tǐ tǎng zài lú huǒ páng biān shuì著 le.
He stretched (himself) out in front of the fire and fell asleep.

他被认为是本世纪第一流的作曲家之一。
tā bèi rèn wéi shì běn shì jì dì yī liú de zuò qǔ jiā zhī yī。
He is regarded as one of the classical composers in this century.

他遭解雇一事, 有关的人都很为难.
tā zāo jiě gù yī shì,  yǒu guān de rén dōu hěn wéi nán.
His dismissal was rather a sticky business for all concerned.

他闪身躲过了滚落的岩石，安然脱险了。
tā shǎn shēn duǒ guò le gǔn luò de yán shí， ān rán tuō xiǎn le。
He dodged the falling rock and escaped unhurt.

他驾驶测验不及格，这次算第十次了。
tā jià shǐ cè yàn bù jí gé， zhè cì suàn dì shí cì le。
That makes the tenth time he's failed his driving test!

仿佛一件小事引起了一连串连锁反应似的。
fǎng fú yī jiàn xiǎo shì yǐn qǐ le yī lián chuàn lián suǒ fǎn yìng sì de。
It is as if a single unimportant event set up a chain of reactions.

你可以用热水把菜盘上凝结的油污冲洗掉。
nǐ kě yǐ yòng rè shuǐ bǎ cài pán shàng níng jié de yóu wū chōng xǐ diào。
You may use hot water to rinse the congealed fat off the dinner plates.

你拿可怜的迈克尔打趣可要出圈儿了.
nǐ ná kě lián de mài kè ěr dǎ qù kě yào chū quān er le.
All your teasing of poor Michael is getting beyond a joke.

你的文章只粗略地涉及到这个问题.
nǐ de wén zhāng zhǐ cū lu:è de shè jí dào zhè gè wèn tí.
Your essay gives a rather sketchy treatment of the problem.

你该知道做这项工作要承担额外责任。
nǐ gāi zhī dào zuò zhè xiàng gōng zuò yào chéng dān é wài zé rèn。
You should know the additional responsibilities that are incidental to the job.

使我惊讶的是，他又犯了同样的错误。
shǐ wǒ jīng yà de shì， tā yòu fàn le tóng yàng de cuò wù。
To my dismay, he made the same mistakes.

公共汽车星期日行驶不一定准能赚钱。
gōng gòng qì chē xīng qī rì xíng shǐ bù yī dìng zhǔn néng zhuàn qián。
It is not always economic for buses to run on Sunday.

决定大选的日期是首相的特权。
jué dìng dà xuǎn de rì qī shì shǒu xiàng de tè quán。
It's the Prime Minister's prerogative to decide when to call an election.

凡是飞机驾驶员均应对乘客的安全负责.
fán shì fēi jī jià shǐ yuán jūn yìng duì chéng kè de ān quán fù zé.
All pilots are responsible for their passengers' safety.

出售枪支受到许多法律限制。
chū shòu qiāng zhī shòu dào xǔ duō fǎ lu:4 xiàn zhì。
The sale of firearms is subject to many legal restrictions.

别把热水倒进玻璃杯里，不然它会炸的。
biè bǎ rè shuǐ dào jìn bō li bēi lǐ， bù rán tā kuài zhà de。
Don't pour hot water into the glass or it will crack.

削减公费开支意味著要砍掉几所医院.
xuē jiǎn gōng fèi kāi zhī yì wèi著 yào kǎn diào jǐ suǒ yī yuàn.
The public spending cuts will mean the chop for several hospitals.

医生们进行会诊，决定是否需要动手术。
yī shēng men jìn xíng kuài zhěn， jué dìng shì fǒu xū yào dòng shǒu zhú。
The doctors held a consultation to decide whether an operation was necessary.

医生告诉他每天饭前吃两片阿斯匹林。
yī shēng gào su tā měi tiān fàn qián jí liǎng piàn ē sī pǐ lín。
The doctor told him to take two tablets of aspirin before every meal.

十二宫图用于占星术中预测未来。
shí èr gōng tú yòng yú zhàn xīng zhú zhòng yù cè wèi lái。
The zodiac is used in astrology to predict the future.

即使我们富裕了也仍应该厉行节约。
jí shǐ wǒ men fù yù le yě réng yīng gāi lì xìng jié yuē。
We should practice economy even if we are rich.

去年是作曲家一生中创作丰收的时期。
qù nián shì zuò qǔ jiā yī shēng zhòng chuàng zuò fēng shōu de shí qī。
Last year was a prolific period in the composer's life.

发射以光线或波的形式发出和传播能量
fā shè yǐ guāng xiàn huò bō de xíng shì fā chū huò chuán bō néng liàng
Emission and propagation of energy in the form of rays or waves.

叙述清楚比语言优美更重要。
xù shù qīng chu bì yǔ yán yōu měi gèng zhòng yào。
Clearness of statement is more important than beauty of language.

哪怕失业，我也要遵循自己的原则。
nǎ pà shī yè， wǒ yě yào zūn xún zì jǐ de yuán zé。
I shall stand by my principles even if it means losing my job.

园艺叉子的一个尖齿把他的脚扎了.
yuán yì chā zi de yī gè jiān chǐ bǎ tā de jué zhá le.
One of the prongs of the garden fork went through his foot.

国际恐怖主义并不是近年才有的现象。
guó jì kǒng bù zhǔ yì bìng bù shì jìn nián cái yǒu de xiàn xiàng。
International terrorism is not just a recent phenomenon.

图上交错的树枝看起来很有诗意。
tú shàng jiāo cuò de shù zhī kàn qǐ lai hěn yǒu shī yì。
The interlacing branches on the picture look poetic.

圣诞节期间生意一向很好.
Shèng dàn jié qī jiān shēng yi yí xiàng hěn hǎo.
Trade is always good (ie Many goods are sold) over the Christmas period.

在一阵痛恨的狂乱中，他杀死了敌人。
zài yī zhèn tòng hèn de kuáng luàn zhòng， tā shā sǐ le dí rén。
In a frenzy of hate he killed his enemy.

在国际市场上，我们的商品不亚于任何人。
zài guó jì shì chǎng shàng， wǒ men de shāng pǐn bù yà yú rèn hé rén。
Our goods are second to none on the world market.

在我们家里，丈夫和我都挣工资。
zài wǒ men jiā lǐ， zhàng fu huò wǒ dōu zhèng gōng zī。
In our family both my husband and I are wage earners.

在有关钱的问题上，我总是尽量小心谨慎。
zài yǒu guān qián de wèn tí shàng， wǒ zǒng shì jìn liàng xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn。
Where money is concerned, I always try to be very careful.

在死者胃中找到了少量的毒药。
zài sǐ zhě wèi zhòng zhǎo dào le shǎo liàng de dú yào。
Small quantities of poison were detected in the dead man's stomach.

在运输中要允许有百分之五的损耗量.
zài yùn shū zhòng yào yǔn xǔ yǒu bǎi fēn zhī wǔ de sǔn hào liàng.
You must allow for five per cent wastage in transit.

地球只是宇宙中众多星球中的一个。
dì qiú zhǐ shì yǔ zhòu zhòng zhòng duō xīng qiú zhòng dì yī gè。
The Earth is only one of the numerous planets in the universe.

处于这种可怕的压力之下，不疯才怪呢。
chǔ yú zhè zhǒng kě pà de yā lì zhī xià， bù fēng cái guài ne。
It's hard to stay sane under such awful pressure.

大声叫嚷的孩子听不到妈妈的叫唤。
dà shēng jiào rǎng de hái zi tìng bù dào mā ma de jiào huan。
The shouting boy did not hear his mother call him.

大群的人迅速地在演说者周围聚集起来。
dà qún de rén xùn sù de zài yǎn shuō zhě zhōu wéi jù jí qǐ lai。
A crowd quickly congregated round the speaker.

奥运会上，他创造了新的世界纪录。
Aò yùn huì shàng， tā chuàng zào le xīn de shì jiè jì lù。
At the Olympic Games, he created a new world record.

奥运会期间，旅馆房间很难找。
Aò yùn huì qī jiān， lu:3 guǎn fáng jiān hěn nàn zhǎo。
Hotel accommodation was scarce during the Olympic Games.

她举起一根手指放在唇边，示意肃静。
tā jǔ qǐ yī gēn shǒu zhǐ fàng zài chún biān， shì yì sù jìng。
She raised her finger to her lips as a sign for silence.

她单凭个人气势就镇住了会场。
tā shàn píng gè rén qì shì jiù zhèn zhù le huì chǎng。
She dominated the meeting by sheer force of character.

她只有坐在壁炉前才感觉到暖和。
tā zhǐ yǒu zuò zài bì lú qián cái gǎn jué dào nuǎn huó。
She felt warm only when she sat before the fireplace.

她宁可辞职也不愿参与这种不正当的买卖.
tā nìng kě cí zhí yě bù yuàn cān yù zhè zhǒng bù zhèng dāng de mǎi mài.
She would sooner resign than take part in such dishonest business deals.

她把她姓名的起首字母绣在手帕上。
tā bǎ tā xìng míng de qǐ shǒu zì mǔ xiù zài shǒu pà shàng。
She embroidered her initials on the handkerchief.

她是个很好的妇人，冷酷不是她的本性。
tā shì gè hěn hǎo de fù rén， lěng kù bú shì tā de běn xìng。
She's a very good woman; unkindness is foreign to her nature.

她的儿子死去时，她悲伤得几乎疯了。
tā de ér zi sǐ qù shí， tā bēi shāng de jī hū fēng le。
She was almost mad with grief when her son died.

她竭力巴结主任希望得到提升.
tā jié lì bā jié zhǔ rèn xī wàng dé dào tí shēng.
She tried to ingratiateherself with the director, in the hope of getting promotion.

如果你不把煤气调小一点，肉就要焦了。
rú guǒ nǐ bù bǎ méi qì tiáo xiǎo yī diǎn， ròu jiù yào jiāo le。
The meat will scorch if you don't lower the gas.

委员会一致同意拒绝这项申请。
wěi yuán huì yī zhì tóng yì jù jué zhè xiàng shēn qǐng。
The committee were unanimous that the application should be turned down.

家庭小商业遭到大公司的吞并.
jiā tíng xiǎo shāng yè zāo dào dà gōng sī de tūn bìng.
Small family businesses are often gobbled up by larger firms.

寒冷的天气终于在三月末结束了。
hán lěng de tiān qì zhōng yú zài sān yuè mò jié shù le。
The cold weather at last broke at the end of March.

对不信上帝的人引用圣经的话是没用的。
duì bù xìn shàng dì de rén yǐn yòng shèng jīng de huà shì méi yòng de。
It's no use citing the Bible to somebody who doesn't believe in God.

对罪犯的改造有了明显的效果。
duì zuì fàn de gǎi zào yǒu le míng xiǎn de xiào guǒ。
The reformation of criminals has produced an obvious result.

小女孩失去了平衡，从平衡木上摔了下来。
xiǎo nu:3 hái shī qù le píng héng， zòng píng héng mù shàng shuāi le xia lai。
The girl lost her balance and fell off the balance beam.

展览会上陈列著所有的新产品。
zhǎn lǎn huì shàng chén liè著 suǒ yǒu de xīn chǎn pǐn。
All the new products are on show at the exhibition.

市外公路上有一处很陡的上坡路。
shì wài gōng lù shang yǒu yī chù hěn dǒu de shàng pō lù。
There was a steep climb on the road out of town.

带动转盘旋转的机械装置坏了.
dài dòng zhuàn pán xuán zhuàn de jī xiè zhuāng zhì huài le.
The mechanism that revolves the turntable is broken.

幕后牵线者如木偶戏中牵金属线或棉线的人
mù hòu qiān xiàn zhě rú mù ǒu xì zhòng qiān jīn shǔ xiàn huò mián xiàn de rén
One who pulls wires or strings, as of puppets.

废除农奴制度后，农奴们获得了解放。
fèi chú nóng nú zhì dù hòu， nóng nú men huò dé liǎo jiě fàng。
The serfs were liberated after abolishing serfdom.

当他跌倒时, 便往一条悬挂的绳子抓去。
dàng tā diē dào shí,  pián wàng yī tiáo xuán guà de shéng zi zhuā qù。
As he fell, he caught hold of a hanging chain.

当年流落他乡的犹太人现在生活在以色列.
dāng nián liú luò tā xiāng de Yóu tài rén xiàn zài shēng huó zài yǐ shǎi liè.
People from every country of the Diaspora now live in Israel.

必须办妥某些手续方可移居他国.
bì xū bàn tuǒ mǒu xiē shǒu xù fāng kě yí jū tā guó.
Certain formalities have to be gone through before one can emigrate.

恋爱与丑闻，是喝茶的最佳甜点心。
liàn ài yù chǒu wén， shì hè chá de zuì jiā tián diǎn xīn。
Love and scandal are the best sweeteners of tea.

我们决定就工资问题与雇主谈判。
wǒ men jué dìng jiù gōng zī wèn tí yù gù zhǔ tán pàn。
We've decided to negotiate with the employers about our wage claim.

我们十几个人像沙丁鱼罐头一样挤成一团。
wǒ men shí jǐ ge rén xiàng shā dīng yú guàn tou yí yàng jǐ chéng yī tuán。
The ten of us were squashed together like sardines in the tin.

我们头顶上的天花板上吊著一盏灯.
wǒ men tou dǐng shàng de tiān huā bǎn shàng diào著 yī zhǎn dēng.
A lamp was suspended from the ceiling above us.

我们得把发动机拆卸开来找出毛病。
wǒ men de bǎ fā dòng jī chāi xiè kāi lái zhǎo chū máo bìng。
We'll have to strip the engine down to find the fault.

我们必须通过智力测验才能被老板雇用。
wǒ men bì xū tōng guò zhì lì cè yàn cái néng bèi lǎo bǎn gù yòng。
We must pass an intelligence test before being hired by the boss.

我们的最终目标是消除所有核武器。
wǒ men de zuì zhōng mù biāo shì xiāo chú suǒ yǒu hé wǔ qì。
Our ultimate objective is the removal of all nuclear weapons.

我们的狗别看样子凶，其实很温顺。
wǒ men de gǒu biè kàn yàng zi xiōng， qí shí hěn wēn shùn。
Our dog may look fierce but he wouldn't hurt a fly.

我们等有空再对这题目展开辩论。
wǒ men děng yǒu kòng zài duì zhè tí mù zhǎn kāi biàn lùn。
We will debate the subject at length later when we are at leisure.

我们都沉浸在春节的欢乐之中。
wǒ men dōu chén jìn zài chūn jié de huān lè zhī zhōng。
We all immersed in the gaiety of the Spring Festival.

我使尽了浑身解数也劝不动他们.
wǒ shǐ jìn le hún shēn xiè shuò yě quàn bù dòng tā men.
I tried every trick in the book but I still couldn't persuade them.

我偶尔喝杯咖啡, 但平常都喝茶.
wǒ ǒu ěr hè bēi kā fēi,  dàn píng cháng dōu hè chá.
I drink an occasional cup of coffee; but usually I take tea.

我可以很清楚地看到灯泡里的细丝断了。
wǒ kě yǐ hěn qīng chu de kàn dào dēng pào lǐ de xì sī duàn le。
I can see clearly that the filament in the bulb is broken.

我对一直放在走廊里的那个包裹有些怀疑。
wǒ duì yī zhí fàng zài zǒu láng lǐ de nèi gè bāo guǒ yǒu xiē huái yí。
I'm a bit suspicious about the package that's been left in the corridor.

我已经决定买一部脚踏车，不论贵不贵。
wǒ yǐ jīng jué dìng mǎi yī bù jué tà jū， bù lùn guì bù guì。
I have decided to buy a bicycle, whether it is expensive or not.

我希望他成为钢琴家的梦想可以成真。
wǒ xī wàng tā chéng wéi gāng qín jiā de mèng xiǎng kě yǐ chéng zhēn。
I hope his dream of becoming a pianist will come true.

我很匆忙, 所以随便地把衣服穿上了。
wǒ hěn cōng máng,  suǒ yǐ suí biàn de bǎ yī fu chuān shàng le。
I was in such a hurry that I put my clothes on anyhow.

我心情愁闷, 不想和任何人讲话。
wǒ xīn qíng chóu mèn,  bù xiǎng huò rèn hé rén jiǎng huà。
I am out of spirits and don't want to speak to anyone.

我想他反正会以养家为理由来进行辩解。
wǒ xiǎng tā fǎn zhèng kuài yǐ yǎng jiā wèi lǐ yóu lái jìn xíng biàn jiě。
I suppose that, in justification, he could always claim he had a family to support.

我把石头搬起来时，那只甲虫跑了。
wǒ bǎ shí tou bān qǐ lai shí， nà zhǐ jiǎ chóng pǎo le。
The beetle scuttled away when I lifted the stone.

我是为那个老人女儿的缘故才照顾他的。
wǒ shì wèi nèi gè lǎo rén nu:3 ér de yuán gù cái zhào gu tā de。
I went to look after the old man on the score of his daughter.

我涂了大量胶水，可那张海报就是贴不住。
wǒ tú le dà liàng jiāo shuǐ， kě nà zhāng hǎi bào jiù shì tiē bú zhù。
The poster wouldn't stick even though I drenched it with glue.

我牙缝里塞了点东西，就是弄不出来。
wǒ yá fèng lǐ sè le diǎn dōng xi， jiù shì nòng bù chū lai。
There is something between my teeth and I can't dislodge it.

我现在辞去主席职位，交由我的副手接替。
wǒ xiàn zài cí qù zhǔ xí zhí wèi， jiāo yóu wǒ de fù shǒu jiē tì。
I am resigning as chairman and handing over to my deputy.

我肚子上挨了一拳一时完全喘不过气来.
wǒ dù zi shàng ái le yī quán yī shí wán quán chuǎn bù guò qì lái.
The punch in the stomach completely winded me.

我请求他从新疆回来时给我带些葡萄干。
wǒ qǐng qiú tā zòng xīn jiāng huí lai shí jǐ wǒ dài xiē pú tao gàn。
I asked him to bring me some raisins when he returns from Xinjiang.

我送给她一条编织的披肩作圣诞礼物。
wǒ sòng jǐ tā yī tiáo biān zhī de pī jiān zuò Shèng dàn lǐ wù。
I gave her a knitted shawl as a Christmas gift.

战胜国要求战败国交付巨额赔款.
zhàn shèng guó yāo qiú zhàn bài guó jiāo fù jù é péi kuǎn.
The victorious nations are demanding huge indemnities from their former enemies.

所有参加辩论的人都有机会发言.
suǒ yǒu cān jiā biàn lùn de rén dōu yǒu jī kuài fā yán.
All the participants in the debate had an opportunity to speak.

手绣的丝制手帕在西方市场销路很好。
shǒu xiù de sī zhì shǒu pà zài xī fāng shì chǎng xiāo lù hěn hǎo。
Silk handkerchiefs embroidered by hand sell well in the Western market.

把无辜的人投入监狱显然是审判不公.
bǎ wú gū de rén tóu rù jiān yù xiǎn ran shì shěn pàn bù gōng.
Sending an innocent man to prison is a clear miscarriage of justice.

据报道，这艘客轮与一艘油轮相撞。
jù bào dào， zhè sōu kè lún yù yī sōu yóu lún xiàng zhuàng。
The liner is reported to have been in collision with an oil tanker.

据说法国人是世界上最好的园丁。
jù shuō fǎ guó rén shì shì jiè shàng zuì hǎo de yuán dīng。
It is said that the Frenchman may be the best gardener in the world.

据说法国人是世界上最浪漫的民族之一。
jù shuō fǎ guó rén shì shì jiè shàng zuì làng màn de mín zú zhī yī。
It is said that Frenchmen are among the most romantic people in the world.

摄政者在他的国家推行了一套先进的制度。
shè zhèng zhě zài tā de guó jiā tuī xíng le yī tào xiān jìn de zhì dù。
The regent carried out an advanced system in his country.

政府声称对失业表示关注纯属做做姿态。
zhèng fǔ shēng chēng duì shī yè biǎo shì guān zhù chún shǔ zuò zuò zī tài。
The government's claim to be concerned about unemployment is sheer hypocrisy.

政府将制定法规限制枪支出售。
zhèng fǔ jiàng zhì dìng fǎ guī xiàn zhì qiāng zhī chū shòu。
The government will introduce legislation to restrict the sale of firearms.

政府已成立工作组调查滥用毒品问题.
zhèng fǔ yǐ chéng lì gōng zuò zǔ diào chá làn yòng dú pǐn wèn tí.
The government has set up a working party to look into the problem of drug abuse.

政府正为处理失业问题的另一计画拨款.
zhèng fǔ zhèng wèi chǔ lǐ shī yè wèn tí de lìng yī jì huà bō kuǎn.
The government is funding another unemployment scheme.

新娘的男亲属们聚集在一起为婚礼做准备。
xīn niáng de nán qīn shǔ men jù jí zài yī qǐ wèi hūn lǐ zuò zhǔn bèi。
The bride's kinsman gathered to make preparations for the wedding.

新来的销售部主任大家还不大了解。
xīn lái de xiāo shòu bù zhǔ rèn dà jiā huán bú dà liǎo jiě。
The new sales director is still a bit of an unknown quantity.

新的住宅区一直延伸到游乐场的那一边.
xīn de zhù zhái qū yī zhí yán shēn dào yóu lè chǎng de nà yī biān.
The new housing estate stretches beyond the playing-fields.

旅馆中的每个房间都有一个单独浴室。
lu:3 guǎn zhòng dì měi gè fáng jiān dōu yǒu yī gè dān dú yù shì。
Every room in the hotel has a private bathroom.

早餐时总统会见了白宫的高级助手.
zǎo cān shí zǒng tǒng huì jiàn le Bái gōng de gāo jí zhù shǒu.
The President met with senior White House aides at breakfast.

最近已经发布了禁止进口毒品的法令。
zuì jìn yǐ jīng fā bù le jìn zhǐ jìn kǒu dú pǐn de fǎ lìng。
A ban on the importation of drugs had been issued recently.

有些罪犯被释放后有可能重新犯罪。
yǒu xiē zuì fàn bèi shì fàng hòu yǒu kě néng chóng xīn fàn zuì。
Some criminals are likely to offend again when they are released.

有几束隐约的阳光使阴暗的下午有些明亮.
yǒu jǐ shù yǐn yuē de yáng guāng shǐ yīn àn de xià wǔ yǒu xiē míng liàng.
A few faint gleams of sunshine lit up the gloomy afternoon.

有很多因素妨碍了我们实现计画.
yǒu hěn duō yīn sù fáng ài le wǒ men shí xiàn jì huà.
Many factors militated against the success of our plan.

根据圣经的说法，我们可以活到七十岁。
gēn jù shèng jīng de shuō fa， wǒ men kě yǐ huó dào qī shí suì。
According to the Bible, we can expect to live for three score years and ten.

桌子接触墙壁的地方漆皮已剥落。
zhuō zi jiē chù qiáng bì de dì fang qī pí yǐ bō luò。
The paint has chipped off where the table touches the wall.

此诗现存最早的原稿收藏在这座博物馆里。
cǐ shī xiàn cún zuì zǎo de yuán gǎo shōu cáng zài zhè zuò bó wù guǎn lǐ。
The earliest extant manuscript of this poem has been kept in the museum.

殖民地人民反抗他们的英国统治者。
zhí mín dì rén mín fǎn kàng tā men de Yīng guó tǒng zhì zhē。
The colonists revolted against their British ruler.

水在穿透岩石的过程中获得了净化.
shuǐ zài chuān tòu yán shí de guò chéng zhòng huò dé le jìng huà.
Water is purified by passing through rock.

污染对这一物种的继续生存造成了威胁。
wū rǎn duì zhè yī wù zhǒng de jì xù shēng cún zào chéng le wēi xié。
Pollution poses a threat to the continued existence of this species.

法律是为保卫人民的权利和财产而制定的。
fǎ lu:4 shì wèi bǎo wèi rén mín de quán lì huò cái chǎn ér zhì dìng de。
Laws are constituted to protect individual rights and properties.

火箭绕地球运行一周后返回基地。
huǒ jiàn rào dì qiú yùn xíng yī zhōu hòu fǎn huí jī dì。
The rocket did one circuit of the earth and returned to base.

炮火掩护步兵前进.
pào huǒ yǎn hù bù bīng qián jìn.
Artillery gave cover (ie fired at the enemy to stop them firing back) while the infantry advanced.

父亲终于与大陆上的弟弟联络上了。

他像是想要人尽心尽力伺候他.
tā xiàng shì xiǎng yào rén jìn xīn jìn lì cì hòu tā.
He seemed to expect to be waited on hand and foot.

他像是想要人尽心尽力伺候他。
tā xiàng shì xiǎng yào rén jìn xīn jìn lì cì hòu tā。
He seems to expect to be wait on hand and foot.

他剪下一串葡萄招待我们。
tā jiǎn xià yī chuàn pú tao zhāo dài wǒ men。
He cut off a bunch of grapes to entertain us.

他受到上司的严厉斥责。
tā shòu dào shàng si de yán lì chì zé。
He received a stern rebuke from his superior.

他哈哈大笑以遮掩紧张的心情.
tā hā hā dà xiào yǐ zhē yǎn jǐn zhāng de xīn qíng.
He laughed to cover (ie hide) his nervousness.

他因品质高尚而被人怀念。
tā yīn pǐn zhì gāo shàng ér bèi rén huái niàn。
He is remembered for the nobility of his character.

他因阻碍公路交通而受控告。
tā yīn zǔ ài gōng lù jiāo tōng ér shòu kòng gào。
He was charged obstructing the highway.

他在事故中大脑受伤无法治愈.
tā zài shì gù zhòng dà nǎo shòu shāng wú fǎ zhì yù.
He suffered irreversible brain damage in the crash.

他在很亮的阳光下眯起了眼睛。
tā zài hěn liàng de yáng guāng xià mǐ qǐ le yǎn jīng。
He squinted in the bright sunlight.

他在自己的领域里已经出名了。
tā zài zì jǐ de lǐng yù lǐ yǐ jīng chū míng le。
He has become famous in his own field.

他坐在摇椅里前后摇晃着。
tā zuò zài yáo yǐ lǐ qián hòu yáo huàng zhuó。
He rocked back and forth in his rocking chair.

他娶了一位非常美丽的姑娘。
tā qǔ le yī wèi fēi cháng měi lì de gū niang。
He married a girl of extraordinary beauty.

他对敌人有强烈的仇恨。
tā duì dí rén yǒu qiáng liè de chóu hèn。
He has a strong animosity against his enemy.

他对文学领域特别感兴趣。
tā duì wén xué lǐng yù tè bié gǎn xìng qu。
His special interest lies in the area of literature.

他尝尝汤, 看是否够咸.
tā cháng cháng tāng,  kàn shì fǒu gòu xián.
He tasted the soup to see if he had put enough salt in it.

他就财产与他们进行商议。
tā jiù cái chǎn yù tā men jìn xíng shāng yì。
He bargained with them for the property.

他很谦虚, 乐于接受意见。
tā hěn qiān xū,  yuè yú jiē shòu yì jiàn。
He is very modest and open to advice.

他心脏停止了跳动, 随即死亡.
tā xīn zàng tíng zhǐ le tiào dòng,  suí jí sǐ wáng.
His heart stopped beating and he died soon afterwards.

他总是叹息研究经费不足。
tā zǒng shì tàn xí yán jiū jīng fèi bù zú。
He always bemoans the shortage of funds for research.

他打开了手电筒，寻找钥匙。
tā dǎ kāi le shǒu diàn tǒng， xún zhǎo yào shi。
He turned on the torch to look for his keys.

他打开了灯，拍松了靠垫。
tā dǎ kāi le dēng， pāi sōng le kào diàn。
He switched on the light and plumped up the cushions.

他打算把财产转让给儿子。
tā dǎ suàn bǎ cái chǎn zhuǎn ràng jǐ ér zi。
He intends to transfer the property to his son.

他把那块石头凿成一个女人像。
tā bǎ nà kuài shí tou zuò chéng yī gè nu:3 rén xiàng。
He chiseled that rock into the figure of a woman.

他抬起头，凝望着天空。
tā tái qǐ tou， níng wàng zhuó tiān kōng。
He rose his head and stared at the firmament.

他撞车后驾驶执照被吊销了。
tā zhuàng chē hòu jià shǐ zhí zhào bèi diào xiāo le。
His driving licence was revoked after the crash.

他是当代医学奇迹的活证明.
tā shì dāng dài yī xué qí jì de huó zhèng míng.
He is living proof of the wonders of modern medicine.

他父亲给他留下了一笔遗产。
tā fù qīn jǐ tā liú xià le yī bǐ yí chǎn。
His father bequeathed him a fortune.

他狠命地抽打那头可怜的驴.
tā hěn mìng de chōu dǎ nà tou kě lián de lu:2.
He gave the poor donkey a terrible lashing.

他猛力一拧, 将那把手拧了下来.
tā měng lì yī nìng,  jiàng nà bǎ shǒu nìng le xia lai.
With a violent twist, he wrenched off the handle.

他用拳头猛击了一下桌子.
tā yòng quán tou měng jī le yī xià zhuō zi.
He struck the table a heavy blow with his fist.

他用蒸汽把信封上的邮票揭下来。
tā yòng zhēng qì bǎ xìn fēng shàng de yóu piào jiē xia lai。
He steamed the stamp off the envelope.

他的名字成了残酷无情的别称.
tā de míng zi chéng le cán kù wú qíng de bié chēng.
His name has becomea byword for cruelty.

他的急躁的脾气使他令人讨厌。
tā de jí zào de pí qì shǐ tā lìng rén tǎo yàn。
His hasty temper made him offensive.

他的患病给我们的计划带来灾难。
tā de huàn bìng jǐ wǒ men de jì huà dài lái zāi nàn。
His illness was fatal to our plan.

他的舌头被红辣椒辣得好难受。
tā de shé tóu bèi hóng là jiāo là de hào nán shòu。
He burned his tongue with red pepper.

他的辩论因被打断而显得不完整。
tā de biàn lùn yīn bèi dǎ duàn ér xiǎn de bù wán zhěng。
The interruption fragmented his argument.

他的陈述促使他们去调查。
tā de chén shù cù shǐ tā men qù diào chá。
His representation influenced them to investigate.

他的鞋子太重，脚上磨出了水泡。
tā de xié zi tài zhòng， jué shàng mò chū le shuǐ pào。
His heavy shoes raised blisters on his feet.

他看著自己的孩子, 充满自豪.
tā kàn著 zì jǐ de hái zi,  chōng mǎn zì háo.
He looked at his children with evident pride.

他研究犯罪心理有多年经验.
tā yán jiū fàn zuì xīn lǐ yǒu duō nián jīng yàn.
He has many years' experience of the criminal mentality.

他突然在冰上摔了个屁股蹲儿。
tā tū rán zài bīng shàng shuāi le gè pì gu dūn er。
Suddenly he sat down on the ice.

他精通世界上的神秘宗教。
tā jīng tōng shì jiè shàng de shén mì zōng jiào。
He is an expert on the world's mystical religions.

他虽然如此年轻，却很慎重。
tā suī rán rú cǐ nián qīng， què hěn shèn zhòng。
Young as he was, he was prudent.

他被任命为驻美国大使。
tā bèi rèn mìng wèi zhù Měi guó dà shǐ。
He was appointed ambassador to the United States.

他被绑在一把椅子上, 就那样待著.
tā bèi bǎng zài yī bǎ yǐ zi shàng,  jiù nà yàng dài著.
He was bound to a chair and left.

他要他们加班工作, 真是残酷。
tā yào tā men jiā bān gōng zuò,  zhēn shì cán kù。
He was cruel to make them work overtime.

他过去的经历笼罩着神秘气氛。
tā guò qu de jīng lì lǒng zhào zhuó shén mì qì fēn。
His past is enveloped in a shroud of mystery.

他那专横的口气激怒了大家。
tā nà zhuān hèng de kǒu qì jī nù le dà jiā。
His peremptory tone irritated everybody.

他靠辛勤劳动而获得成功.
tā kào xīn qín láo dòng ér huò dé chéng gōng.
His success was achieved by hard work.

他驾驶考试合格使大家很惊奇.
tā jià shǐ kǎo shì hé gé shǐ dà jiā hěn jīng qí.
He amazed everyone by passing his driving test.

会议遭示威者干扰而结束.
huì yì zāo shì wēi zhě gān rǎo ér jié shù.
The meeting was closed after the demonstrators interrupted it.

你不可因一个人贫穷而轻视他。
nǐ bù kě yīn yī gè rén pín qióng ér qīng shì tā。
You must not despise a man because he is poor.

你不能毫无根据地逮捕他。
nǐ bù néng háo wú gēn jù dì dài bǔ tā。
You shouldn't arrest him without warrant.

你可以在银行开立一个活期帐户。
nǐ kě yǐ zài yín háng kāi lì yī gè huó qī zhàng hù。
You may open a current account at a bank.

你可以接通全国计算机网络。
nǐ kě yǐ jiē tōng quán guó jì suàn jī wǎng luò。
You can plug into the national computer network.

你得雇个人监督这一工程.
nǐ de gù gè rén jiān dū zhè yī gōng chéng.
You must employ someone to oversee the project.

你离家不归, 你母亲极为伤心.
nǐ lí jiā bù guī,  nǐ mǔ qīn jí wéi shāng xīn.
Your mother is very grieved by your refusal to return home.

使人发狂的官僚主义的混乱状况
shǐ rén fā kuáng de guān liáo zhǔ yì de hùn luàn zhuàng kuàng
Maddening bureaucratic mix-ups.

保险公司将赔偿他的损失。
bǎo xiǎn gōng sī jiàng péi cháng tā de sǔn shī。
The insurance company will recompense his loss.

信中夹钞票最好寄挂号.
xìn zhòng jiá chāo piào zuì hǎo jì guà hào.
It's wise to register letters containing banknotes.

候选人在辩论中唇枪舌箭。
hòu xuǎn rén zài biàn lùn zhòng chún qiāng shé jiàn。
The candidates exchanged shafts in the debate.

做纵横字谜游戏能锻炼脑筋.
zuò zòng héng zì mí yóu xì néng duàn liàn nǎo jīn.
Doing crosswords gives the mind some exercise.

做饭的味道顺着走廊飘过来。
zuò fàn de wèi dao shùn zhuó zǒu láng piāo guò lai。
Cooking smells wafted along the hall.

元旦那天他们都感到宿醉头痛。
yuán dàn nà tiān tā men dōu gǎn dào xiù zuì tóu tòng。
On New Year's Day they were all hung over.

入侵者把村镇变为废墟。
rù qīn zhě bǎ cūn zhèn biàn wèi fèi xū。
The invader laid towns and villages in ruins.

全城沉浸在节日的气氛中。
quán chéng chén jìn zài jié rì de qì fēn zhòng。
The whole city was immersed in a festival atmosphere.

六十岁时, 他开始学俄语。
liù shí suì shí,  tā kāi shǐ xué é yǔ。
At the age of sixty he took up the study of Russian.

兼职音乐教师定期到校授课.
jiān zhí yīn yuè jiào shī dìng qī dào xiào shòu kè.
Peripatetic music teachers visit the school regularly.

再向前展望到本世纪末....
zài xiàng qián zhǎn wàng dào běn shì jì mò....
Looking farther forward to the end of the century...

出版社侵犯了他的版权。
chū bǎn shè qīn fàn le tā de bǎn quán。
The publishing house infringed his copyright.

别在快餐馆耽误太长时间。
biè zài kuài cān guǎn dān wu tài cháng shí jiān。
Don't stay too long at the snack bar.

动物的粪便可以作为肥料使用。
dòng wù de fèn biàn kě yǐ zuò wéi féi liào shǐ yòng。
Animal dung may be used as manure.

北方的大荒原地广人稀。
běi fāng de dà huāng yuán de guǎng rén xī。
The wasteland of the north is scarcely populated.

去年癌症夺走了他姐姐的生命。
qù nián ái zhèng duó zǒu le tā jiě jie de shēng mìng。
Cancer carried his sister off last year.

参加聚会的男子大都非常年轻。
cān jiā jù huì de nán zǐ dà dōu fēi cháng nián qīng。
The men at the party were mostly fairly young.

向悲观的人推销保险很容易.
xiàng bēi guān de rén tuī xiāo bǎo xiǎn hěn róng yì.
It's easy to sell insurance to a pessimist.

向顶峰攀登时身上都热起来了。
xiàng dǐng fēng pān dēng shí shēn shàng dōu rè qǐ lai le。
It was a warm climb to the summit.

因为滥用权力，他被开除了。
yīn wèi làn yòng quán lì， tā bèi kāi chú le。
Because of misuse of power, he was dismissed.

园丁向我要一台旋转式割草机。
yuán dīng xiàng wǒ yào yī tái xuán zhuǎn shì gē cǎo jī。
The gardener asked me for a rotatory lawn mower.

固定物牢固地安放在一个地方的东西
gù dìng wù láo gù de ān fàng zài yī gè dì fang de dōng xi
Something securely fixed in place.

圣诞礼物都用薄纸裹起来了.
Shèng dàn lǐ wù dōu yòng bó zhǐ guǒ qǐ lai le.
The Christmas presents were wrapped (up) in tissue paper.

圣诞节我们度过了一个狂欢之夜。
Shèng dàn jié wǒ men dù guò le yī gè kuáng huān zhī yè。
We spent a riotous night at Christmas.

在公共汽车上要谨防扒手。
zài gōng gòng qì chē shàng yào jǐn fáng pá shǒu。
Please guard against pickpockets on the bus.

在动物园我看见了两只小骆驼。
zài dòng wù yuán wǒ kàn jiàn le liǎng zhǐ xiǎo luò tuo。
I saw two small camels in the zoo.

在旧社会老百姓的生活是贫苦的
zài jiù shè huì lǎo bǎi xìng de shēng huó shì pín kǔ de
The husbandmen's life in old society is poor.

在英国，车辆必须靠左行驶。
zài Yīng guó， chē liàng bì xū kào zuǒ xíng shǐ。
In England traffic must keep to the left.

地震对这个城市造成了大破坏。
dì zhèn duì zhè gè chéng shì zào chéng le dà pò huài。
The earthquake wreaked havoc on the city.

垂直线与水平线在此相交.
chuí zhí xiàn yù shuǐ píng xiàn zài cǐ xiāng jiāo.
The vertical line meets the horizontal one here.

墙壁因地震而倾斜。
qiáng bì yīn dì zhèn ér qīng xié。
The wall declined slightly on account of the earthquake.

声波是根据其振幅来测量的.
shēng bō shì gēn jù qí zhèn fú lái cè liàng de.
Sound waves are measured by their amplitude.

太阳照耀着美丽的城市。
tài yáng zhào yào zhuó měi lì de chéng shì。
The sun shine bright in the beautiful city.

奇迹是与大自然的力量相对的.
qí jì shì yù dà zì rán de lì liang xiāng duì de.
Miracles are contrary to nature.

她仍然坚持要求赔偿.
tā réng rán jiān chí yāo qiú péi cháng.
She is still pressing her claim for compensation.

她佩戴了一把小梳子作为装饰品。
tā pèi dài le yī bǎ xiǎo shū zi zuò wéi zhuāng shì pǐn。
She wore a small comb as an ornament.

她兼做导师工作和研究工作.
tā jiān zuò dǎo shī gōng zuò huò yán jiū gōng zuò.
Her work was divided between tutoring and research.

她出于情感的缘故做了此事。
tā chū yú qíng gǎn de yuán gù zuò le cǐ shì。
She did it for sentimental reasons.

她出于虚荣心而嫁给了那个富人。
tā chū yú xū róng xīn ér jià jǐ le nèi gè fù rén。
She married the rich man out of vanity.

她加入了大学里的艺术协会。
tā jiā rù le dà xué lǐ de yì shù xié huì。
She joined the university art society.

她匆匆忙忙向电报局去了。
tā cōng cōng máng máng xiàng diàn bào jú qù le。
She went to the telegraph office in a hurry.

她发觉地毯下面有许多尘土.
tā fā jué dì tǎn xià mian yǒu xǔ duō chén tǔ.
She found a lot of dust underneath the carpet.

她听到这一悲惨消息, 脸都白了.
tā tīng dào zhè yī bēi cǎn xiāo xi,  liǎn dōu bái le.
She listened to the tragic news ashen-faced.

她喘著气好不容易才说出了几个字来.
tā chuǎn著 qì hào bù róng yì cái shuō chū le jǐ ge zì lái.
She managed to gasp (out) a few words.

她在铝锅里下了些面条。
tā zài lu:3 guō lǐ xià le xiē miàn tiáo。
She put some noodles in the aluminum saucepan.

她姿色迷人，因而评委都偏向她。
tā zī sè mí rén， yīn ér píng wěi dōu piān xiàng tā。
Her charm prejudiced the judges in her favour.

她很聪明, 倒也很谦虚.
tā hěn cōng míng,  dào yě hěn qiān xū.
Though very intelligent, she is nevertheless rather modest.

她很高兴去掉了这个包袱。
tā hěn gāo xìng qù diào le zhè gè bāo fu。
She was glad to be relieved of this burden.

她忍气吞声地继续进行下去。
tā rěn qì tūn shēng de jì xù jìn xíng xià qu。
She swallowed her anger and carried on.

她把窗台漆上鲜艳的颜色。
tā bǎ chuāng tái qī shàng xiān yàn de yán sè。
She painted the window sills a bright colour.

她把葡萄放到一个大盘子上。
tā bǎ pú tao fàng dào yī gè dà pán zi shàng。
She put the grapes onto the platter.

她把食物和饮料放在客人面前。
tā bǎ shí wù huò yǐn liào fàng zài kè ren miàn qián。
She set the foods and drink before the guest.

她挣扎著想摆脱那个侵犯她的人.
tā zhēng zhá著 xiǎng bǎi tuō nèi gè qīn fàn tā de rén.
She struggled to get away from her attacker.

她是位眼光敏锐的艺术评论家.
tā shì wèi yǎn guāng mǐn ruì de yì shù píng lùn jiā.
She is a very discerning art critic.

她的勤奋为其他人树立了榜样。
tā de qín fèn wèi qí tā rén shù lì le bǎng yàng。
Her diligence has set an example to the others.

她的合伙人企图骗走她的股份。
tā de hé huǒ rén qǐ tú piàn zǒu tā de gǔ fèn。
Her partner tried to trick her out of her share.

她的声音中能听出有些颤抖.
tā de shēng yīn zhòng néng tìng chū yǒu xiē chàn dǒu.
You could hear the quaver in her voice.

她的懒丈夫成了她的一个包袱。
tā de lǎn zhàng fu chéng le tā de yī gè bāo fu。
Her lazy husband is a millstone round her neck.

她的智慧比我们猜想的要高。
tā de zhì huì bì wǒ men cāi xiǎng de yào gāo。
She has more intelligence than we suspected her to possess.

她的眼里流露出受委屈的神情.
tā de yǎn lǐ liú lù chū shòu wěi qū de shén qíng.
Her eyes took on a hurt expression.

她看样子随时都可能垮下来.
tā kàn yàng zi suí shí dōu kě néng kuǎ xia lai.
She looked ready to collapse at any minute.

她眼睛里闪烁著调皮的光辉.
tā yǎn jīng lǐ shǎn shuò著 tiáo pí de guāng huī.
Her eyes twinkled with mischief.

她竭力争取自己想要的东西。
tā jié lì zhēng qǔ zì jǐ xiǎng yào de dōng xi。
She fought like a tiger to get what she wanted.

她自豪地看著自己的工作成果.
tā zì háo de kàn著 zì jǐ de gōng zuò chéng guǒ.
She looked with pride at the result of her work.

她让我吃些药片以利睡眠.
